</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Length</th><td class="infobox-data plainlist"><span class="duration"><span class="min">4</span>:<span class="s">26</span></span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label"><a href="/wiki/Record_label" title="Record label">Label</a></th><td class="infobox-data hlist"><a href="/wiki/Work_Records" class="mw-redirect" title="Work Records">Work</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/Songwriter" title="Songwriter">Songwriter(s)</a></span></th><td class="infobox-data hlist">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Rodney_Jerkins" title="Rodney Jerkins">Rodney Jerkins</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/LaShawn_Daniels" title="LaShawn Daniels">LaShawn Daniels</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cory_Rooney" title="Cory Rooney">Cory Rooney</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez" title="Jennifer Lopez">Jennifer Lopez</a></li>
<li>Fred Jerkins III</li></ul>
</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/Record_producer" title="Record producer">Producer(s)</a></span></th><td class="infobox-data hlist">Rodney Jerkins</td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" class="infobox-header description" style="background-color: khaki;"><a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez" title="Jennifer Lopez">Jennifer Lopez</a> singles chronology</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" class="infobox-full-data">
<table style="background: transparent; width: 100%; min-width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse;">

<tbody><tr style="line-height: 1.4em;">
<td style="width: 33%; text-align: center; vertical-align: top; padding: .2em .1em .2em 0;">
</td>
<td style="width: 33%; text-align: center; vertical-align: top; padding:.2em .1em;">"<b>If You Had My Love</b>" <br>(1999)
</td>
<td style="width: 33%; text-align: center; vertical-align: top; padding: .2em 0 .2em .1em;">"<a href="/wiki/No_Me_Ames" title="No Me Ames">No Me Ames</a>" <br>(1999)
</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>"If You Had My Love"</b> is a song recorded by American actress and singer <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez" title="Jennifer Lopez">Jennifer Lopez</a>. It was released on May 4, 1999, as the lead single from her debut studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/On_the_6" title="On the 6">On the 6</a></i> (1999). The song was written by <a href="/wiki/LaShawn_Daniels" title="LaShawn Daniels">LaShawn Daniels</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cory_Rooney" title="Cory Rooney">Cory Rooney</a>, Jennifer Lopez, Fred Jerkins III, and its producer <a href="/wiki/Rodney_Jerkins" title="Rodney Jerkins">Rodney Jerkins</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> "If You Had My Love" is a midtempo <a href="/wiki/Pop_music" title="Pop music">pop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Contemporary_R%26B" title="Contemporary R&amp;B">R&amp;B</a> song that also features <a href="/wiki/Latin_music_(genre)" class="mw-redirect" title="Latin music (genre)">Latin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hip_hop_music" title="Hip hop music">hip hop</a> influences. Its lyrics revolve around the beginning of a new relationship, during which Lopez confronts her admirer with a number of ground rules.
</p><p>Critics reacted positively to "If You Had My Love", praising its "silky groove" and "edgy" production.<sup id="cite_ref-Johnson_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Johnson-3">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_Review_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_Review-4">[4]</a></sup> Upon its release, it generated instant attention and became a commercial success, peaking at number one on the US <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a> for five weeks. It became one of the best-selling singles of 1999, selling over 1.2 million units in the US alone. It was also an international success, topping the charts in Australia, Canada, Finland, Greece, Hungary and New Zealand. Its success came as a surprise to critics, making Lopez one of few actors to successfully crossover into the <a href="/wiki/Music_industry" title="Music industry">music industry</a>. It also contributed to the growing popularity of Latin artists in Northern America. In retrospect, "If You Had My Love" has been described as an "R&amp;B classic",<sup id="cite_ref-DS_2012_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DS_2012-5">[5]</a></sup> and it is considered one of Lopez's best songs.
</p><p>The song's accompanying <a href="/wiki/Music_video" title="Music video">music video</a> (directed by <a href="/wiki/Paul_Hunter_(director)" title="Paul Hunter (director)">Paul Hunter</a>) features a voyeuristic internet concept, wherein Lopez's spectators are able to direct her through <a href="/wiki/Cyberspace" title="Cyberspace">cyberspace</a>. The provocative video received heavy rotation on <a href="/wiki/MTV" title="MTV">MTV</a> networks internationally, allowing Lopez to "push the envelope" in a field that was primarily dominated by <a href="/wiki/Janet_Jackson" title="Janet Jackson">Janet Jackson</a> and <a href="/wiki/Madonna_(entertainer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Madonna (entertainer)">Madonna</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Asia_Pacific_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Asia_Pacific-6">[6]</a></sup> The clip was nominated for four <a href="/wiki/MTV_Video_Music_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="MTV Video Music Award">MTV Video Music Awards</a> and five <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Music_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Billboard Music Award">Billboard Music Awards</a>. Lopez promoted the song through performances at the <a href="/wiki/Blockbuster_Entertainment_Awards" title="Blockbuster Entertainment Awards">Blockbuster Entertainment Awards</a> and VH1/Vogue Fashion Awards in 1999. She has subsequently performed it on a number of occasions, including her <a href="/wiki/Let%27s_Get_Loud_(concerts)" title="Let's Get Loud (concerts)">Let's Get Loud</a> concerts in 2001, and her <a href="/wiki/Dance_Again_World_Tour" title="Dance Again World Tour">Dance Again World Tour</a> in 2012, where she performed an acoustic version of the song. It also serves as the opening number to her Las Vegas residency show, <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez:_All_I_Have" title="Jennifer Lopez: All I Have">Jennifer Lopez: All I Have</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>After a series of co-starring film roles, Lopez had her breakthrough when she was cast in the title role of <i><a href="/wiki/Selena_(film)" title="Selena (film)">Selena</a></i> (1997), a biographical film about American singer-songwriter <a href="/wiki/Selena" title="Selena">Selena</a> Quintanilla-Prez.<sup id="cite_ref-SMH_2014_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SMH_2014-7">[7]</a></sup> Working on the film inspired her to launch a music career, with Lopez saying: "I started my career in musical theater on stage. So doing the movie just reminded me of how much I missed singing, dancing, and the like..." After filming <i>Selena,</i> Lopez was "really feeling [her] Latin roots" and recorded a demo record in Spanish.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> Her manager sent the song ("Vivir Sin Ti") to <a href="/wiki/Sony_Music_Entertainment" class="mw-redirect" title="Sony Music Entertainment">Sony Music Entertainment</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Work_Group" title="Work Group">Work Group</a>, which was interested in signing Lopez. <a href="/wiki/Tommy_Mottola" title="Tommy Mottola">Tommy Mottola</a>, the head of the label, suggested that she sing in English and she began recording her debut album, <i><a href="/wiki/On_the_6" title="On the 6">On the 6</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> Her decision to launch a musical career was seen as a risk, as film stars had a "patchy record" when it came to releasing pop music,<sup id="cite_ref-SMH_2014_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SMH_2014-7">[7]</a></sup> and "If the album was a flop, not only would it embarrass Lopez but it might even damage her career."<sup id="cite_ref-Latin_Sensations_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Latin_Sensations-10">[10]</a></sup> Lopez originally believed that "<a href="/wiki/Feelin%27_So_Good" title="Feelin' So Good">Feelin' So Good</a>" was to be released as the album's lead single.<sup id="cite_ref-Feelin'_So_Good_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Feelin'_So_Good-11">[11]</a></sup> "If You Had My Love" was produced by <a href="/wiki/Rodney_Jerkins" title="Rodney Jerkins">Rodney Jerkins</a>; Lopez recorded her vocals for the song at <a href="/wiki/Sony_Music_Studios" title="Sony Music Studios">Sony Music Studios</a> in <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a> with engineers Franklyn Grant and Robb Williams. The song was later <a href="/wiki/Mix_engineer" class="mw-redirect" title="Mix engineer">mixed</a> by Tony Maserati at <a href="/wiki/The_Hit_Factory" title="The Hit Factory">The Hit Factory</a> in New York City, and subsequently <a href="/wiki/Audio_mastering" class="mw-redirect" title="Audio mastering">mastered</a> by Herb Powers at Powers House of Sound.<sup id="cite_ref-Production_Credits_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Production_Credits-12">[12]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-EU_maxi_single_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EU_maxi_single-13">[13]</a></sup> Shawnyette Harrell and Jennifer Karr served as backing vocalists.<sup id="cite_ref-ot6_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ot6-14">[14]</a></sup>
</p><p>According to <a href="/wiki/Cory_Rooney" title="Cory Rooney">Cory Rooney</a>, one of the song's co-writers, Lopez was almost finished recording <i>On the 6</i> when Rooney and Jerkins played a CD playlist of songs for <a href="/wiki/Michael_Jackson" title="Michael Jackson">Michael Jackson</a>, which included "If You Had My Love." Rooney believed the song was "perfect for Jennifer", and hoped that Jackson would not take it. Rooney recalled: "The music begins and Michael starts moving and shaking to it and he goes, 'Man, I like this one.' My heart sunk. Then he says, 'I dont like it for me, but I like it. It's gonna be a hit for someone else.'"<sup id="cite_ref-Cory_Rooney_Latina_Interview_2016_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cory_Rooney_Latina_Interview_2016-15">[15]</a></sup> Rooney said that he and <a href="/wiki/LaShawn_Daniels" title="LaShawn Daniels">LaShawn Daniels</a> wrote "If You Had My Love" later that day.<sup id="cite_ref-Cory_Rooney_Latina_Interview_2016_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cory_Rooney_Latina_Interview_2016-15">[15]</a></sup> Conversely, journalist Damien Shields stated in 2015 that Rooney had Lopez record the song in 1998, and that it had already been allocated to her when Jackson heard it. Jackson thought it had a "really great groove" and briefly considered recording it. Shields said: "Everyone's like, 'Shit, now were going to have to argue with the King of Pop because that's already going to be Jennifer's first song and it's already in motion and is going to radio in two months.' How do you possibly tell Michael Jackson no?"<sup id="cite_ref-Damien_Shields_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Damien_Shields-16">[16]</a></sup> Jackson passed on the song, believing it was better suited for a female singer. "It was the only one of Rodney's songs that he gravitated towards, but he also had the intuition to know that a female should sing it for it realize its best potential," Shields noted.<sup id="cite_ref-Damien_Shields_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Damien_Shields-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p><p>"If You Had My Love" became the subject of some controversy when it emerged that Jerkins had written a "nearly identical song" for singer <a href="/wiki/Chant%C3%A9_Moore" title="Chant Moore">Chant Moore</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SMH_2014_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SMH_2014-7">[7]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Rolling_Stone_2014_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rolling_Stone_2014-17">[17]</a></sup> Moore asserted that her song "If I Gave Love" was re-written with the same arrangement for Lopez after it was requested by <a href="/wiki/Sean_Combs" title="Sean Combs">Sean Combs</a>, one of <i>On the 6</i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">'</span>s producers. Moore said: "He wrote the same song for her. I heard that it was because Puff Daddy walked in and heard my song and said 'I want that song,' and he [Rodney] was like 'Well that's already taken. We wrote that for Chante,' and he was like 'I want that song.' So Rodney wrote, really, the same song."<sup id="cite_ref-CBS_Radio_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CBS_Radio-18">[18]</a></sup> "If I Gave Love" was intended to be released as a single from her album <i><a href="/wiki/This_Moment_Is_Mine" title="This Moment Is Mine">This Moment Is Mine</a></i> (1999), but was ultimately scrapped before Lopez recorded her version.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Composition">Composition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Composition">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>"If You Had My Love" is a mid-tempo <a href="/wiki/Pop_music" title="Pop music">pop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Contemporary_R%26B" title="Contemporary R&amp;B">R&amp;B</a> song with a length of four minutes and twenty-five seconds (4:25),<sup id="cite_ref-Johnson_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Johnson-3">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LA_Times_99_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LA_Times_99-20">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AllMusic_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AllMusic-21">[21]</a></sup> which contains elements of <a href="/wiki/Salsa_music" title="Salsa music">salsa</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hip_hop" title="Hip hop">hip hop</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Johnson_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Johnson-3">[3]</a></sup> The song was written and composed mainly by <a href="/wiki/Rodney_Jerkins" title="Rodney Jerkins">Rodney Jerkins</a>, <a href="/wiki/LaShawn_Daniels" title="LaShawn Daniels">LaShawn Daniels</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cory_Rooney" title="Cory Rooney">Cory Rooney</a>, with Lopez herself contributing<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="Please clarify the preceding statement or statements with a good explanation from a reliable source. (November 2017)">how?</span></a></i>]</sup> to the lyrics; Jerkins also served as producer.<sup id="cite_ref-ot6_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ot6-14">[14]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Cory_Rooney_Latina_Interview_2016_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cory_Rooney_Latina_Interview_2016-15">[15]</a></sup> It is written in the <a href="/wiki/Key_(music)" title="Key (music)">key</a> of <a href="/wiki/B_minor" title="B minor">B minor</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Tempo" title="Tempo">tempo</a> of 94 beats per minute. The instrumentation of "If You Had My Love" consists of a <a href="/wiki/Piano" title="Piano">piano</a> and <a href="/wiki/Guitar" title="Guitar">guitar</a>. Lopez's vocals in the song span from the lower note of <a href="/wiki/A%E2%99%AF_(musical_note)" title="A (musical note)">A<sub>3</sub></a> to the higher note of <a href="/wiki/E%E2%99%AF_(musical_note)" class="mw-redirect" title="E (musical note)">E<sub>5</sub></a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Musicnotes_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Musicnotes-22">[22]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/BBC_Music" title="BBC Music">BBC Music</a> writer Michael Cragg remarked that her vocals possessed a "cooing innocence".<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> Beth Johnson of <i><a href="/wiki/Entertainment_Weekly" title="Entertainment Weekly">Entertainment Weekly</a></i> described the song as "slow-<a href="/wiki/Funk" title="Funk">funk</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-Johnson_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Johnson-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small-left noprint" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000;float:left">

<td class="mbox-image"><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/50px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="50" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/75px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/100px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="160" data-file-height="160"></div></div></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist" style="line-height:1.1em"><div class="haudio">
<div style="padding:4px 0"><a href="/wiki/File:If_You_Had_My_Love_(Edit).ogg" title="File:If You Had My Love (Edit).ogg">"If You Had My Love"</a></div>
<div><div class="mediaContainer" style="width:220px"><div class="mwPlayerContainer k-player" style="width: 220px; position: relative; height: 20px;"><div class="videoHolder"><div class="mwEmbedPlayer" id="mwe_player_0" style=""><img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVR42mNkqAcAAIUAgUW0RjgAAAAASUVORK5CYII=" class="playerPoster" style="position: absolute; inset: 0px 0px 0px 100px; height: 20px; width: 20px;"></div><div title="Play clip" class="play-btn-large" style="left: 50%; top: 50%; margin-left: -35px; margin-top: -27.5px;"></div></div><div class="ui-state-default ui-widget-header ui-helper-clearfix control-bar block" style="height: 20px;"><div title="Player options" class="ui-state-default ui-corner-bl rButton k-options"><span>Menu</span></div><div class="ui-slider ui-slider-horizontal rButton volume-slider ui-widget ui-widget-content ui-corner-all"><div class="ui-slider-range ui-widget-header ui-slider-range-min" style="width: 80%;"></div><a class="ui-slider-handle ui-state-default ui-corner-all" href="#" style="left: 80%;"></a></div><div title="Volume control" class="ui-state-default ui-corner-all ui-icon_link rButton volume_control"><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-volume-on"></span></div><div title="Timed text" class="ui-state-default ui-corner-all ui-icon_link rButton timed-text"><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-comment"></span></div><div class="ui-widget time-disp">0:00</div><div title="Play clip" class="ui-state-default ui-corner-all ui-icon_link lButton play-btn"><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-play"></span></div></div></div></div></div>
<div class="description" style="padding:2px 0 0 0">A twenty second sample of "If You Had My Love," featuring "lust-leery" lyrics<sup id="cite_ref-Vibe_2000_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vibe_2000-24">[24]</a></sup> through which Lopez "questions the nature of her beau's affections."<sup id="cite_ref-MTV_Vena_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MTV_Vena-25">[25]</a></sup></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td colspan="2" class="mbox-text" style="line-height:1.1em"><hr><i class="selfreference">Problems playing this file? See <a href="/wiki/Help:Media" title="Help:Media">media help</a>.</i></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>Lyrically, the song resembles a conversation, in which Lopez confronts her admirer in an "insistent" manner with a number of ground rules before they can begin a relationship.<sup id="cite_ref-AllMusic_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AllMusic-21">[21]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MTV_News_2011_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MTV_News_2011-26">[26]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/MTV_News" title="MTV News">MTV</a>'s James Dinh said Lopez "lets her insecurities get the best of her" on the track.<sup id="cite_ref-MTV_News_2011_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MTV_News_2011-26">[26]</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> writer Leslie Richin wrote that it "served as a cautionary tale for admirers who might one day have a chance with the budding starlet. Bottom line: liars and cheaters need not apply."<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_2015_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_2015-27">[27]</a></sup> In the song's opening lines, Lopez states: "Now if I gave you me, this is how it's got to be / First of all I won't take you cheatin' on me / Tell me who can I trust if I can't trust in you / And I refuse to let you play me for a fool."<sup id="cite_ref-MTV_News_2011_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MTV_News_2011-26">[26]</a></sup> In the chorus, she poses the question: "If you had my love / And I gave you all my trust... / Would you lie to me / And call me baby?"<sup id="cite_ref-Vibe_2000_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vibe_2000-24">[24]</a></sup> Lopez explained in her book <i><a href="/wiki/True_Love_(book)" title="True Love (book)">True Love</a></i> (2014) that the lyrics refer to "the beginning of a new relationship and what I expect and what I want," saying that "there's a little bit of fear in there too, and a feeling of, what will you do if I give you my heart?"<sup id="cite_ref-True_Love_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-True_Love-28">[28]</a></sup> The verses consist of her "trying to lay down the rules", while the chorus expresses "all of the fear" that she feels.<sup id="cite_ref-True_Love_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-True_Love-28">[28]</a></sup> Jocelyn Vena of MTV News noted that "If You Had My Love" marked the beginning of Lopez exploring the topic of love, which she has continued throughout her career.<sup id="cite_ref-MTV_Vena_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MTV_Vena-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Critical_reception">Critical reception</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Critical reception">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>"If You Had My Love" was received positively by <a href="/wiki/Music_journalism" title="Music journalism">music critics</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Official_Charts_2015_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Official_Charts_2015-29">[29]</a></sup> In a review of <i>On the 6,</i> <i><a href="/wiki/NME" title="NME">NME</a></i> noted that Lopez "really comes into her own" on the song, describing it as one of the album's "street-smart swingbeat winners".<sup id="cite_ref-NME_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NME-30">[30]</a></sup> Chuck Taylor of <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> spoke favorably of the song's production, calling it "contemporary and edgy, straight down the <a href="/wiki/Faith_Evans" title="Faith Evans">Faith Evans</a> pathway," but noted that its melody was similar to that of "<a href="/wiki/The_Boy_Is_Mine_(song)" title="The Boy Is Mine (song)">The Boy Is Mine</a>," another song written and composed by Jerkins. Taylor wrote, "Lopez seems to have command of the most important elementher voicethough admittedly, the vocal melody of this song holds tightly to a very narrow edge. Lopez might remind listeners of the funkier side of <a href="/wiki/Vanessa_Williams" title="Vanessa Williams">Vanessa Williams</a> [...] Curiosity alone will propel this onto the pop and R&amp;B airwaves; at that point, the hook, along with an undoubtedly compelling video clip, should take this debut far."<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_Review_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_Review-4">[4]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/AllMusic" title="AllMusic">AllMusic</a>'s Heather Phares said that it has a "fiery, soulful sound more in keeping with Lopez's public persona."<sup id="cite_ref-AllMusic_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AllMusic-21">[21]</a></sup> Aaron Beierle of <a href="/wiki/DVD_Talk" title="DVD Talk">DVD Talk</a> praised the song as "catchy," writing that it "showcases the singer's style well."<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup>
</p><p>Beth Johnson of <i>Entertainment Weekly</i> was also favorable, noting the song to feature a "silky groove". Johnson also observed: "Considering the dustbins filled with movie stars' vanity discs, why expect this actress' recording debut to be hit-bound? Well, surprise, surprise."<sup id="cite_ref-Johnson_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Johnson-3">[3]</a></sup> Elysa Gardner of the <i><a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Times" title="Los Angeles Times">Los Angeles Times</a></i> described the track as an "exotic hip hop" workout.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Vibe_(magazine)" title="Vibe (magazine)">Vibe</a></i> magazine writer Dream Hampton called the song "sweet" and "upbeat", and commented on Lopez's "strong" vocals.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> Brian McCollum of the <i><a href="/wiki/Rome_News-Tribune" title="Rome News-Tribune">Rome News-Tribune</a></i> called "If You Had My Love" one of the year's most "infectious" singles.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup> Amy Sciarretto of <a href="/wiki/PopCrush" class="mw-redirect" title="PopCrush">PopCrush</a> praised it as a "silky-smooth", "confident" song that "established her as more than just an actress who was 'dabbling' in music [...] Her voice may be thin, but she chose a song that worked with her vocal limitations. It's [a] semi-synthy, mid-tempo, contempo R&amp;B pop that's flawlessly executed."<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup> A reporter from the <i><a href="/wiki/International_Business_Times" title="International Business Times">International Business Times</a></i> called the song "radio-friendly".<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup> In a review of Lopez's remix album <i><a href="/wiki/J_to_tha_L%E2%80%93O!_The_Remixes" title="J to tha LO! The Remixes">J to tha LO! The Remixes</a></i> (2002), Sal Cinquemani of <i><a href="/wiki/Slant_Magazine" title="Slant Magazine">Slant Magazine</a></i> praised the Dark Child remix of "If You Had My Love," which utilized a "delectable" interpolation of Michael Jackson's "<a href="/wiki/Liberian_Girl" title="Liberian Girl">Liberian Girl</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup>
</p><p>But Jerome Joseph, also from the <i>Los Angeles Times,</i> was not as positively receptive of the single, arguing that it sounded like a "<a href="/wiki/Brandy_Norwood" title="Brandy Norwood">Brandy</a> or <a href="/wiki/Monica_(singer)" title="Monica (singer)">Monica</a> reject", and called Lopez "<a href="/wiki/Paula_Abdul" title="Paula Abdul">Paula Abdul</a> 2000".<sup id="cite_ref-Joseph_2000_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Joseph_2000-38">[38]</a></sup> Similarly, <i><a href="/wiki/Hartford_Courant" title="Hartford Courant">Hartford Courant</a></i> writer Roger Catlin stated that the song is "more of a bland R&amp;B number that could have been sung by anybody", suggesting that it has "little Latin flair".<sup id="cite_ref-Catlin_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Catlin-39">[39]</a></sup> While Scott Iwasald of <i><a href="/wiki/Deseret_News" title="Deseret News">Deseret News</a></i> characterized Lopez's vocals as "sultry" but thin, he noted that she finds a "nice ring" in songs such as "If You Had My Love".<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/1999_Teen_Choice_Awards" title="1999 Teen Choice Awards">1999 Teen Choice Awards</a>, the song won the award for "Song of the Summer".<sup id="cite_ref-BMI_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BMI-41">[41]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Chart_performance">Chart performance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Chart performance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Following its release on May 11, 1999, the song garnered instant radio attention.<sup id="cite_ref-Official_Charts_2015_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Official_Charts_2015-29">[29]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_January_2000_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_January_2000-42">[42]</a></sup> Promotional images relating to the single featured Lopez in "seductive poses" and "skin tight clothing". <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> commented that the Work Group was "taking every advantage of her sexy image to aid the marketing side."<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_Review_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_Review-4">[4]</a></sup> "If You Had My Love" debuted at number 72 on the US <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a> for the week ending May 15, 1999, and moved to number 64 in its second week.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> The following week, the song sold 66,000 copies, debuting at number five on the Hot 100 Singles Sales chart. This, along with a 16.7% increase in radio audience, allowed it to rise to number eight on the Hot 100; it also reached the top ten of the <a href="/wiki/Hot_R%26B/Hip-Hop_Songs" title="Hot R&amp;B/Hip-Hop Songs">Hot R&amp;B/Hip-Hop Songs</a> chart this week.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup> In its fourth week, the song rose to number one on the Hot 100 Singles Sales, with 120,000 units sold during the week (representing an 80% increase in sales). It subsequently moved to number two on the Hot 100, earning the "Greatest Gainer" title of the week.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup>
</p><p>For the week of June 12, 1999, "If You Had My Love" reached number one on the Hot 100. It experienced 30% increase in sales and an airplay increase of 5.6 million in audience impressions.<sup id="cite_ref-billboardno1issue_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-billboardno1issue-46">[46]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup> The song displaced <a href="/wiki/Ricky_Martin" title="Ricky Martin">Ricky Martin</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/Livin%27_La_Vida_Loca" class="mw-redirect" title="Livin' La Vida Loca">Livin' La Vida Loca</a>" on the Hot 100, which was the first time a Latin artist followed another Latin artist to the top of the chart since <a href="/wiki/Gloria_Estefan" title="Gloria Estefan">Gloria Estefan</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/Coming_Out_of_the_Dark" title="Coming Out of the Dark">Coming Out of the Dark</a>" replaced <a href="/wiki/Timmy_T" title="Timmy T">Timmy T</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/One_More_Try_(Timmy_T._song)" class="mw-redirect" title="One More Try (Timmy T. song)">One More Try</a>" in March 1991. Lopez became the first artist to top the <i>Billboard</i> Hot 100 with their debut single since <a href="/wiki/Britney_Spears" title="Britney Spears">Britney Spears</a> did so with her single, "<a href="/wiki/...Baby_One_More_Time_(song)" title="...Baby One More Time (song)">...Baby One More Time</a>" just four months prior. Furthermore, "If You Had My Love" gave the <a href="/wiki/Work_Group" title="Work Group">WORK Group</a> its first number one hit on the chart.<sup id="cite_ref-billboardno1issue_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-billboardno1issue-46">[46]</a></sup> In its sixth week, the song sold a further 170,500 copies. This week, "If You Had My Love" became the second song in the magazine's history to be number one on the Hot 100 and be the "Greatest Gainer" in both sales and airplay, after "Livin' La Vida Loca" in May.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup> In addition, the song also became the first in <i>Billboard</i> history to claim to number one position on the Hot 100, Hot 100 Singles Sales and R&amp;B Singles Sales charts simultaneously.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup>
</p><p>For the week ending July 17, 1999, the song fell to number two on the Hot 100, having been dethroned by <a href="/wiki/Destiny%27s_Child" title="Destiny's Child">Destiny's Child</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/Bills,_Bills,_Bills" title="Bills, Bills, Bills">Bills, Bills, Bills</a>." Despite this, it reached its highest radio audience to date this week, with 84.2 million listeners.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup> It spent five weeks at number one on the Hot 100,<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup> tying with <a href="/wiki/Christina_Aguilera" title="Christina Aguilera">Christina Aguilera</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/Genie_in_a_Bottle" title="Genie in a Bottle">Genie in a Bottle</a>" for the longest-running number one hit of the summer.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup> "If You Had My Love" remained in the top ten until September 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> The song would also peak at number two on the US <a href="/wiki/Mainstream_Top_40_(Pop_Songs)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mainstream Top 40 (Pop Songs)">Pop Songs</a> chart, six on Hot R&amp;B/Hip-Hop Songs and five on <a href="/wiki/Hot_Dance_Club_Play" class="mw-redirect" title="Hot Dance Club Play">Hot Dance Club Play</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ifyou3_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ifyou3-54">[54]</a></sup> It was the sixth best-selling song in the US of 1999 with 1.2 million copies sold,<sup id="cite_ref-Year_End_Sales_1999_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Year_End_Sales_1999-55">[55]</a></sup> and was certified platinum by <a href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_America" title="Recording Industry Association of America">RIAA</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BMI_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BMI-41">[41]</a></sup> In 2015, <i>Billboard</i> ranked it as the second biggest hit of the summer of 1999, behind "Genie in a Bottle".<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup>
</p><p>The song debuted and peaked at number four on the <a href="/wiki/UK_Singles_Chart" title="UK Singles Chart">UK Singles Chart</a>, selling 77,000 copies in its first week. It became the first of Lopez's 17 top ten hits in that country.<sup id="cite_ref-Official_Charts_2015_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Official_Charts_2015-29">[29]</a></sup> By 2016, it had sold 366,000 copies in the United Kingdom.<sup id="cite_ref-Official_Charts_2016_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Official_Charts_2016-57">[57]</a></sup> "If You Had My Love" reached number one in Australia, and was certified platinum by the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Recording_Industry_Association" title="Australian Recording Industry Association">Australian Recording Industry Association</a> for shipments of 70,000 units.<sup id="cite_ref-aus_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-aus-58">[58]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AustraliaPlatinum_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AustraliaPlatinum-59">[59]</a></sup> It also topped the charts in New Zealand,<sup id="cite_ref-newz_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-newz-60">[60]</a></sup> Canada,<sup id="cite_ref-canada_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-canada-61">[61]</a></sup> the Netherlands<sup id="cite_ref-nether_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nether-62">[62]</a></sup> and Finland.<sup id="cite_ref-fin_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fin-63">[63]</a></sup> In France, it was certified gold by the <a href="/wiki/Syndicat_National_de_l%27%C3%89dition_Phonographique" title="Syndicat National de l'dition Phonographique">Syndicat National de l'dition Phonographique</a> for shipments of 100,000 units.<sup id="cite_ref-goldfrance_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goldfrance-64">[64]</a></sup> It was also certified gold in Germany, Switzerland, and New Zealand.<sup id="cite_ref-germany1_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-germany1-65">[65]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-nzc_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nzc-66">[66]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-swiz_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-swiz-67">[67]</a></sup> Reflecting on the song's success in 2011, Lopez said, "Still I think about that and still it's like wow, my first record I ever did went to number one. It's just an overwhelming feeling. This does not happen all the time. This is a very special thing."<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup> As of 2017, the single has sold over 5 million copies worldwide.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Music_video">Music video</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Music video">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Production">Production</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Production">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Adam_Rodr%C3%ADguez_February_2015.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Adam_Rodr%C3%ADguez_February_2015.jpg/150px-Adam_Rodr%C3%ADguez_February_2015.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="225" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Adam_Rodr%C3%ADguez_February_2015.jpg/225px-Adam_Rodr%C3%ADguez_February_2015.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Adam_Rodr%C3%ADguez_February_2015.jpg/300px-Adam_Rodr%C3%ADguez_February_2015.jpg 2x" data-file-width="311" data-file-height="467"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Adam_Rodr%C3%ADguez_February_2015.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Actor <a href="/wiki/Adam_Rodriguez" title="Adam Rodriguez">Adam Rodriguez</a> appears in the music video.</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Music_video" title="Music video">music video</a> for "If You Had My Love" was directed by <a href="/wiki/Paul_Hunter_(director)" title="Paul Hunter (director)">Paul Hunter</a>. It features a <a href="/wiki/Voyeuristic" class="mw-redirect" title="Voyeuristic">voyeuristic</a> internet theme, wherein a range of viewers watch Lopez through webcams by accessing "Jennifer Lopez Online".<sup id="cite_ref-LA_Times_99_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LA_Times_99-20">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_2015_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_2015-27">[27]</a></sup> The <i>Los Angeles Times</i> described it as a "timely thematic fusion of elaborate dance numbers, the voyeurism of the Internet and Lopez's raw powers of attraction on men, women and little girls." The "interactive" music video was launched in junction with Lopez's own official website at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-LA_Times_99_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LA_Times_99-20">[20]</a></sup> Its "voyeuristic quality" was Hunter's idea, while <a href="/wiki/Sean_Combs" title="Sean Combs">Sean Combs</a> came up with the website concept that "tied it all together". Lopez, who had a specific idea of how she wanted the dance break to be, described the music video as a collaboration between herself, Hunter, Combs, and her manager <a href="/wiki/Benny_Medina" title="Benny Medina">Benny Medina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Feelin'_So_Good_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Feelin'_So_Good-11">[11]</a></sup> The clip debuted on the May 17, 1999, edition of <i><a href="/wiki/Total_Request_Live" title="Total Request Live">Total Request Live</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup> and was serviced to music video outlets for the week ending May 22, 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup> Actor <a href="/wiki/Adam_Rodriguez" title="Adam Rodriguez">Adam Rodriguez</a>, who appears in the music video, said: "Jennifer and I were friends when she called me up to do her video [...] I remember thinking, Why not just do it? Then it turned out that the single was a massive hit and what really catapulted her career to global fame. To be a part of that made it a fun summer because everybody knew that video."<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[72]</a></sup> Lopez's outfits and accessories in the music video included a white bikini top and low rise sweatpants,<sup id="cite_ref-Cosmopolitan_Outfit_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cosmopolitan_Outfit-73">[73]</a></sup> a "plunging" gold necklace,<sup id="cite_ref-Latina_Outfit_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Latina_Outfit-74">[74]</a></sup> and a mini mirror dress during one of the dance sequences.<sup id="cite_ref-BET_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BET-75">[75]</a></sup> In it, she also sported a sleek hairstyle with honey highlights.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synopsis">Synopsis</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Synopsis">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:If_You_Had_My_Love.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c0/If_You_Had_My_Love.jpg/220px-If_You_Had_My_Love.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="129" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c0/If_You_Had_My_Love.jpg/330px-If_You_Had_My_Love.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/c/c0/If_You_Had_My_Love.jpg 2x" data-file-width="412" data-file-height="242"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:If_You_Had_My_Love.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The music video centers around a "Welcome to Jennifer Lopez Online" concept.<sup id="cite_ref-Idolator_2014_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Idolator_2014-77">[77]</a></sup></div></div></div>
<p>The clip begins in a dark room, where a man (Rodriguez) searches "Jennifer Lopez" on his computer and is redirected to her website<sup id="cite_ref-LN_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LN-78">[78]</a></sup> (which is displayed by special effects emulating <a href="/wiki/Binary_numeral_system" class="mw-redirect" title="Binary numeral system">binary numbers</a>). He views a live feed of Lopez in her home, which is filled with cameras.<sup id="cite_ref-Complex_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Complex-79">[79]</a></sup> She appears in a number of settings, including a living room and crawling over a table, and is visibly aware of the viewers, waving to the camera before the song begins. The man is not alone in his voyeuristic actions, as patrons of an internet caf, a little girl in her bedroom, and Latin women in their kitchen among others are also streaming a live feed of Lopez through computers and <a href="/wiki/Internet_television" class="mw-redirect" title="Internet television">internet television</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-LN_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LN-78">[78]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Complex_79-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Complex-79">[79]</a></sup> Viewers are able to select where Lopez is located in cyberspace from a range of options. The man clicks on a room showing Lopez in the bathroom, singing whilst checking her reflection in the mirror.<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_2015_27-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_2015-27">[27]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LN_78-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LN-78">[78]</a></sup>
</p><p>Lopez's feed is also being streamed live to a nightclub and a call center. The man then clicks on the dance option and is once again entered through the special effect binary. Lopez proceeds to perform a series of dances (including jazz, <a href="/wiki/House_music" title="House music">house</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Latin_soul" title="Latin soul">Latin soul</a>) as the song moves into a <a href="/wiki/Remix" title="Remix">remixed</a> (Pablo Flores Remix) portion.<sup id="cite_ref-LN_78-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LN-78">[78]</a></sup> The man then zooms in on Lopez's skirt, as she dances to Latin music. He then raises the sexual intonation again by requesting a scene in which Lopez is taking a shower.<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_2015_27-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_2015-27">[27]</a></sup> A pair of mechanics who had been watching this soon turn their heads to Lopez and pay no attention to their burning car as they glue their eyes to the screen.<sup id="cite_ref-LN_78-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LN-78">[78]</a></sup> A new user is introduced, and it is implied that he throws his computer underwater to "turn down the heat" (so to speak), where he continues to watch her. In the original ending, Rodriguez is shown running his left hand underneath his shirt and "sucking his right hand's fingers" while Lopez looks at him through the camera while in the shower. This footage was cut from the final version.<sup id="cite_ref-CBS_Radio_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CBS_Radio-18">[18]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Reception_and_impact">Reception and impact</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Reception and impact">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Following its release, the "body-emphasizing" music video was played in heavy rotation on <a href="/wiki/MTV" title="MTV">MTV</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> called it "<a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/muy" class="extiw" title="wikt:muy">muy</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/caliente" class="extiw" title="wikt:caliente">caliente</a>" and a "fantasy",<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_2015_27-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_2015-27">[27]</a></sup> and <i><a href="/wiki/Vibe_(magazine)" title="Vibe (magazine)">Vibe</a></i> named it one of her best dance videos.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup> In 2015, <a href="/wiki/BET" title="BET">BET</a> wrote, "We dont think anyone can forget Jennifer's saucy dance number from her debut video."<sup id="cite_ref-BET_75-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BET-75">[75]</a></sup> According to monitoring by <a href="/wiki/Nielsen_Broadcast_Data_Systems" class="mw-redirect" title="Nielsen Broadcast Data Systems">Nielsen Broadcast Data Systems</a>, the clip became the most played on <a href="/wiki/VH1" title="VH1">VH1</a> at one point in August 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup> In August 1999, a writer from <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> discussed the video's international impact, writing that Lopez "isn't too far behind Ricky Martin as the leading light of Latin music in Asia. On the strength of the video for 'If You Had My Love,' Lopez has skyrocketed from an unknown to superstar status in markets as diverse as the Philippines and India."<sup id="cite_ref-Asia_Pacific_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Asia_Pacific-6">[6]</a></sup> Jeff Selamutu, a programming manner from <a href="/wiki/Channel_V" title="Channel V">Channel V</a>, opined that Lopez "really pushed the envelope for international female artists" in the Asia-Pacific region, noting: "Up to now, it's only been <a href="/wiki/Janet_Jackson" title="Janet Jackson">Janet Jackson</a> and <a href="/wiki/Madonna_(entertainer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Madonna (entertainer)">Madonna</a>." As a result, Channel V structured a month-long campaign around the release of <i>On the 6,</i> with "If You Had My Love" being played up to six times a day on the network's international feeds.<sup id="cite_ref-Asia_Pacific_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Asia_Pacific-6">[6]</a></sup> In 2014, Christina Lee of <a href="/wiki/Idolator_(website)" title="Idolator (website)">Idolator</a> described the video as "classic Jennifer," saying: "The way Jennifer would stare into the camera  that was effortless [...] One moment she's tough, with her hard stares and insistent lyrics [...] But then she pivots her hips and sneaks a casual smile over her shoulder. She was both a diva and down-to-earth."<sup id="cite_ref-Idolator_2014_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Idolator_2014-77">[77]</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Nine.com.au" title="Nine.com.au">Nine.com.au</a> called the music video's <a href="/wiki/Cyberstalking" title="Cyberstalking">cyberstalking</a> vibe "creepy",<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup> with <i><a href="/wiki/Complex_(magazine)" class="mw-redirect" title="Complex (magazine)">Complex</a></i> magazine regarding the video as one of the "Greatest Tech Moments in Music Video History".<sup id="cite_ref-Complex_79-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Complex-79">[79]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Lisa_Nakamura" title="Lisa Nakamura">Lisa Nakamura</a> analyzed the video in her book <i>Digitizing Race: Visual Cultures of the Internet</i> (2008), noting that it "puts a new spin on the traditional female position as object of the gaze", where Lopez presents herself "as an objective of interactivity". Nakamura added: "In this video we have access to the star's body through the viewer's mind. We see her as he sees her, through interface use. This split represents a paradigmatic dichotomy in gender theory: the body is that of the Latina, the woman of color, and the mind is that of a white man."<sup id="cite_ref-LN_78-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LN-78">[78]</a></sup> In <i>Rewind, Play, Fast Forward: The Past, Present and Future of the Music Video</i> (2015), authors Henry Keazor and Thorsten Wbbena observed that "the idea of an online presence of a musical star was conceived and visualized" in the video, writing: "the singer was presented as a sort of 'belle captive' (as one could put it by quoting the title of a novel by <a href="/wiki/Alain_Robbe-Grillet" title="Alain Robbe-Grillet">Alain Robbe-Grillet</a>), because she seems to be confined to a series of white, clinical rooms where everything is under observation." The authors also noted that the video foreshadowed "the reality as it was viewable" through the <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a> phenomenon.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup> Justin Myers of the <a href="/wiki/Official_Charts_Company" title="Official Charts Company">Official Charts Company</a> said that the "reality TV-inspired video" which predated the UK version of <i><a href="/wiki/Big_Brother_(UK_TV_series)" class="mw-redirect" title="Big Brother (UK TV series)">Big Brother</a></i> in fact resembled the first series, calling this "J-Lo's #impact".<sup id="cite_ref-Official_Charts_2016_57-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Official_Charts_2016-57">[57]</a></sup> In 2021, American rapper <a href="/wiki/Princess_Nokia" title="Princess Nokia">Princess Nokia</a> paid homage to the video in her own music video for "It's Not My Fault", in which she recreated Lopez's look and a number of scenes from "If You Had My Love".<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup> 
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Fuse.tv" class="mw-redirect" title="Fuse.tv">Fuse.tv</a> included "If You Had My Love" among Lopez's most iconic music video looks.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup> Monica Castillo of <i><a href="/wiki/Cosmopolitan_(magazine)" title="Cosmopolitan (magazine)">Cosmopolitan</a></i> called Lopez's outfit "inexplicably sexy",<sup id="cite_ref-Cosmopolitan_Outfit_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cosmopolitan_Outfit-73">[73]</a></sup> while <i><a href="/wiki/Latina_(magazine)" title="Latina (magazine)">Latina</a></i> magazine writer Nichole Fratangelo said she "looked angelic in white but of course, she gave it a naughty twist."<sup id="cite_ref-Latina_Outfit_74-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Latina_Outfit-74">[74]</a></sup> Gaby Wilson of <a href="/wiki/MTV_News" title="MTV News">MTV News</a> highlighted the video's influence in <a href="/wiki/Selena_Gomez" title="Selena Gomez">Selena Gomez</a>'s video for "<a href="/wiki/Slow_Down_(Selena_Gomez_song)" title="Slow Down (Selena Gomez song)">Slow Down</a>", stating that it was similar to Lopez "dancing solo in that clinically white/silver space".<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/1999_MTV_Video_Music_Awards" title="1999 MTV Video Music Awards">1999 MTV Video Music Awards</a>, the video received four nominations, including <a href="/wiki/Best_Female_Video" class="mw-redirect" title="Best Female Video">Best Female Video</a>, <a href="/wiki/Best_Dance_Video" class="mw-redirect" title="Best Dance Video">Best Dance Video</a>, <a href="/wiki/Best_Pop_Video" class="mw-redirect" title="Best Pop Video">Best Pop Video</a> and <a href="/wiki/MTV_Video_Music_Award_for_Best_New_Artist" class="mw-redirect" title="MTV Video Music Award for Best New Artist">Best New Artist in a Video</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Asia_Pacific_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Asia_Pacific-6">[6]</a></sup> At the 1999 Billboard Music Video Awards, "If You Had My Love" was nominated for the Maximum Vision Award, Best Dance Clip, Best New Artist Dance Clip, Best Pop Clip and Best New Artist Pop Clip. Lopez was the artist with the most nominations that year.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Live_performances">Live performances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Live performances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:JLO_43_-_BERCY_-_OCTOBRE_2012_(8097659485).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/JLO_43_-_BERCY_-_OCTOBRE_2012_%288097659485%29.jpg/200px-JLO_43_-_BERCY_-_OCTOBRE_2012_%288097659485%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="266" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/JLO_43_-_BERCY_-_OCTOBRE_2012_%288097659485%29.jpg/300px-JLO_43_-_BERCY_-_OCTOBRE_2012_%288097659485%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/JLO_43_-_BERCY_-_OCTOBRE_2012_%288097659485%29.jpg/400px-JLO_43_-_BERCY_-_OCTOBRE_2012_%288097659485%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2653" data-file-height="3527"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:JLO_43_-_BERCY_-_OCTOBRE_2012_(8097659485).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Lopez performing an acoustic version of "If You Had My Love" during her <a href="/wiki/Dance_Again_World_Tour" title="Dance Again World Tour">Dance Again World Tour</a> in 2012.</div></div></div>
<p>Lopez performed "If You Had My Love" at the 5th <a href="/wiki/Blockbuster_Entertainment_Awards" title="Blockbuster Entertainment Awards">Blockbuster Entertainment Awards</a> which were held on June 26, 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-Feelin'_So_Good_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Feelin'_So_Good-11">[11]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup> That December, she performed the <a href="/wiki/Darkchild" class="mw-redirect" title="Darkchild">Darkchild</a> remix of the song at the VH1/Vogue Fashion Awards, where she also won the award for "Fashionable Female Artist."<sup id="cite_ref-Feelin'_So_Good_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Feelin'_So_Good-11">[11]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup> In September 2001, performed it again during her <a href="/wiki/Let%27s_Get_Loud_(concerts)" title="Let's Get Loud (concerts)">Let's Get Loud</a> concerts in Puerto Rico, which were her first full shows.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup>
</p><p>Lopez included "If You Had My Love" on the set list of her 2007 <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez_and_Marc_Anthony_en_Concierto" class="mw-redirect" title="Jennifer Lopez and Marc Anthony en Concierto">co-headlining concert tour</a> with then-husband <a href="/wiki/Marc_Anthony" title="Marc Anthony">Marc Anthony</a>, which was her first tour.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup> At her October 2011 <a href="/wiki/Mohegan_Sun" title="Mohegan Sun">Mohegan Sun</a> concert celebrating the casino's 15th anniversary, Lopez performed an acoustic version of "If You Had My Love." The stage was lit by blue and surrounded by dry-ice smoke,<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup> with Lopez asking the audience, "You want to talk about love?" as she introduced the song.<sup id="cite_ref-EW_2011_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW_2011-97">[97]</a></sup> It was reported that Lopez "broke down" in tears after the performance.<sup id="cite_ref-EW_2011_97-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW_2011-97">[97]</a></sup> Lopez once again performed a "stripped down" acoustic version of the song throughout her 2012 <a href="/wiki/Dance_Again_World_Tour" title="Dance Again World Tour">Dance Again World Tour</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-THR_2012_98-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-THR_2012-98">[98]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup> Describing it as the "first real intimate moment of the show," she wanted to perform a "pared down" version of the song so that it would feel like a conversation, "like I'm talking with the audience, sharing where I began and where I find myself now."<sup id="cite_ref-True_Love_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-True_Love-28">[28]</a></sup> Gerrick Kennedy of the <i><a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Times" title="Los Angeles Times">Los Angeles Times</a></i> wrote that while "Live ballads still aren't firmly in her wheelhouse," she "sounded best" during the acoustic performance.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">[100]</a></sup> Michele Amabile Angermiller of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hollywood_Reporter" title="The Hollywood Reporter">The Hollywood Reporter</a></i> called the performance "a sweet and intimate moment," adding: "Sometimes, simply delivering a song without all the bells and whistles is enough."<sup id="cite_ref-THR_2012_98-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-THR_2012-98">[98]</a></sup>
</p><p>At the <a href="/wiki/Dubai_World_Cup" title="Dubai World Cup">Dubai World Cup</a> in March 2014, Lopez performed a <a href="/wiki/Striptease" title="Striptease">striptease</a> in which she had "If You Had My Love" woven in with her song "<a href="/wiki/Girls_(Jennifer_Lopez_song)" title="Girls (Jennifer Lopez song)">Girls</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup> She described the performance as <a href="/wiki/Burlesque" title="Burlesque">burlesque</a>-esque.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup> "If You Had My Love" serves at the opening number in her Las Vegas residency, <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez:_All_I_Have" title="Jennifer Lopez: All I Have">Jennifer Lopez: All I Have</a>, which commenced in 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LAT_2016_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LAT_2016-104">[104]</a></sup> The performance was preceded by an "ethereal, fairy-tale overture," where female dancers in showgirl costumes were suspended above the stage. Lopez wore a crystal-encrusted sparkly bodysuit and a white feathered robe.<sup id="cite_ref-LAT_2016_104-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LAT_2016-104">[104]</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> writer Eve Barlow called it a "dazzling opening."<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup> The song was also incorporated into the striptease segment later in the show, where she "writhed around a chaise lounge."<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup>
</p><p>Lopez performed the "Pablo Flores Remix" version of the song as part of her medley during the <a href="/wiki/2018_MTV_Video_Music_Awards" title="2018 MTV Video Music Awards">2018 MTV Video Music Awards</a> on August 20, 2018 at <a href="/wiki/Radio_City_Music_Hall" title="Radio City Music Hall">Radio City Music Hall</a> in <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Impact">Impact</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=If_You_Had_My_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Impact">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Jennifer_Lopez_12,_2012.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Jennifer_Lopez_12%2C_2012.jpg/200px-Jennifer_Lopez_12%2C_2012.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="228" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Jennifer_Lopez_12%2C_2012.jpg/300px-Jennifer_Lopez_12%2C_2012.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Jennifer_Lopez_12%2C_2012.jpg/400px-Jennifer_Lopez_12%2C_2012.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2581" data-file-height="2947"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Jennifer_Lopez_12,_2012.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Lopez performing an acoustic version of "If You Had My Love" during her Dance Again World Tour in 2012.</div></div></div>
<p>Following the release of "If You Had My Love," which according to <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> was preceded by a "hype storm that has clapped like thunder for months",<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_Review_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_Review-4">[4]</a></sup> Lopez rose to international visibility and was propelled to pop stardom,<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_January_2000_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_January_2000-42">[42]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup> emerging as a "certifiable pop star".<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup> The <i><a href="/wiki/New_York_Daily_News" title="New York Daily News">New York Daily News</a></i> noted that "the world knew that J.Lo was something special."<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Radar_Online" title="Radar Online">Radar Online</a> stated that she "became a pop sensation overnight".<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup> While she had already achieved notability as an actress, the song's success is what made Lopez a household name.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup> The release of "If You Had My Love" and <i>On the 6</i> allowed Lopez to join an "elite circle" of actors who had successfully crossed over to music, becoming the first since <a href="/wiki/Vanessa_L._Williams" class="mw-redirect" title="Vanessa L. Williams">Vanessa Williams</a> in 1992 and <a href="/wiki/Martika" title="Martika">Martika</a> in 1989.<sup id="cite_ref-billboardno1issue_46-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-billboardno1issue-46">[46]</a></sup> In 2008, <a href="/wiki/News.com.au" title="News.com.au">News.com.au</a> wrote that the transition from actress to singer "has always been a precarious career path, claiming many victims", identifying Lopez as one of the "success stories that keep a steady stream of actresses attempting to make that career crossover." The website also wrote: "For every success story there are more than a handful of failures, or in celebrity-to-celebrity ratio, one Jennifer Lopez to three <a href="/wiki/Minnie_Driver" title="Minnie Driver">Minnie Drivers</a>."<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone" title="Rolling Stone">Rolling Stone</a></i> noted that the single marked the beginning of Lopez's own media empire.<sup id="cite_ref-Rolling_Stone_2014_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rolling_Stone_2014-17">[17]</a></sup> Writing for <i><a href="/wiki/Dazed" title="Dazed">Dazed</a>,</i> Kat George opined that Lopez was celebrity <a href="/wiki/Feminism" title="Feminism">feminist</a>, a premise that was defined by "If You Had My Love," which had a "succinct and demanding message about womanhood".<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup>
</p><p>The success of "If You Had My Love," which was considered unlikely,<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup> coincided with the "Latin explosion" of 1999, which was led by <a href="/wiki/Ricky_Martin" title="Ricky Martin">Ricky Martin</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Catlin_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Catlin-39">[39]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BMI_41-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BMI-41">[41]</a></sup> Some critics assumed that Lopez was attempting to capitalize on the growing popularity of Latin music in the United States. Her subsequent success on the charts came as a surprise to critics; Hern Marquez wrote in <i>Latin Sensations</i> (2001) that it "made the popular actor even more popular. Suddenly, the music industry and the public were intrigued by this woman who seemed to have so many different talents."<sup id="cite_ref-Latin_Sensations_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Latin_Sensations-10">[10]</a></sup> Chris Poppe, vice president of marketing for <a href="/wiki/Epic_Records" title="Epic Records">Epic Records</a>, noted: "It was easy for the media to lump Jennifer into that, even though this is technically not a Latin album. It drew a lot of positive attention to 'If You Had My Love'. Radio reacted almost immediately to the song." Jennifer Charles from <a href="/wiki/KSZR" title="KSZR">KSZR</a> said, "If you had doubts about the idea of Jennifer Lopez as a recording artist, they were gone once the groove kicked in and she started to sing."<sup id="cite_ref-Billboard_January_2000_42-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Billboard_January_2000-42">[42]</a></sup> The interest in Martin and Lopez was further credited with "boosting the profile of Latin music in Canada", and helped <a href="/wiki/Sony_Music" title="Sony Music">Sony Music</a> Entertainment Canada launch another singer, <a href="/wiki/Marc_Anthony" title="Marc Anthony">Marc Anthony</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-billboardno1issue_46-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-billboardno1issue-46">[46]</a></sup>
</p><p>Considered iconic,<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup> a number of sources have listed "If You Had My Love" as one of Lopez's best songs. <i><a href="/wiki/Complex_(magazine)" class="mw-redirect" title="Complex (magazine)">Complex</a></i> magazine named the song her greatest hit in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">[118]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/About.com" class="mw-redirect" title="About.com">About.com</a> music journalist Bill Lamb ranked it as Lopez's best song, praising its "elegant feel laced with surging strings."<sup id="cite_ref-About.com_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-About.com-119">[119]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/AOL_Radio" title="AOL Radio">AOL Radio</a> listeners also chose it as her best song.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">[120]</a></sup> Stacy Lambe of <a href="/wiki/VH1" title="VH1">VH1</a> listed the song as Lopez's fifth best single, writing: "Lopez's debut single drew on everything that was popular in 1999. It fused together the synths made popular by <a href="/wiki/TLC_(group)" title="TLC (group)">TLC</a>, highlighted the Latin flare made profitable by <a href="/wiki/Ricky_Martin" title="Ricky Martin">Ricky Martin</a> and came packaged with Lopez's movie brand recognition and sex appeal. The pop song did what it was supposed to do, debuting at number 1 on the <i>Billboard</i> Hot 100 and announcing that Jennifer the singer had arrived."<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Bustle_(magazine)" title="Bustle (magazine)">Bustle</a></i> magazine writer Jordana Lipsitz called it one of the defining songs of the summer of 1999, adding: "This song was the jam you and your gal pals practiced your back up dancer routines with. Admit it."<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone" title="Rolling Stone">Rolling Stone</a></i> included the song on a list of the "20 Biggest Songs of the Summer" from the 1990s.<sup id="cite_ref-Rolling_Stone_2014_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rolling_Stone_2014-17">[17]</a></sup> In 2012, Lewis Corner of <i><a href="/wiki/Digital_Spy" title="Digital Spy">Digital Spy</a></i> described "If You Had My Love" as an "R&amp;B classic", which serves as "a firm reminder of her fiercely independent but hopeless romantic nature, which seems to reflect her colourful personal life."<sup id="cite_ref-DS_2012_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DS_2012-5">[5]</a></sup> Rapper <a href="/wiki/T-Pain" title="T-Pain">T-Pain</a> stated that it was the Darkchild remix of "If You Had My Love", which he recalled used <a href="/wiki/Auto-Tune" title="Auto-Tune">Auto-Tune</a> "for like a second", that inspired his use of the pitch correction processor.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Canadian recording artist <a href="/wiki/Drake_(musician)" title="Drake (musician)">Drake</a> sampled the song's chorus in "Teenage Fever," a song from his playlist <i><a href="/wiki/More_Life" title="More Life">More Life</a></i> (2017).<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">[124]</a></sup> American singer, <a href="/wiki/Melanie_Martinez" title="Melanie Martinez">Melanie Martinez</a> sampled the song on Brain and Heart off her <i><a href="/wiki/After_School_(EP)" title="After School (EP)">After School</a></i> EP, released in 2020.
</p>
